 in mulakaaton se kayaas lagaae rahe hai ki kya narendra modi or amit shah kii mukhar aalochak raheen banerjee ke rukh main narmi aa gayi he

 ' isi twit ke saath unhone modi or shah se banerjee kii mulaakaat kii do tasviren bhi post kii hai or likhaa he ki modi or shah se banerjee kii mulaakaat ko kya is arth main liya jaae? kuch din pehle, vijayawargeey ne kaha tha ki banerjee kii modi se mulaakaat kolkata ke purv police ayukta rajeev kumaar ko bachaane kii aakhri koshish he

 Mamta said, 'meeting the Prime Minister and Home Minister is a constitutional obligation
 iske alaava hamaare paas bangladesh or bhutan ke saath lagati antarrashtriya seemaa ko lekar mudde hai tathaa bihar or jharkhand ke saath rajya kii lagati seemaa ko lekar bhi mudde hai
